<time>1551813145098</time><rate>4</rate>< text>
Korean Town in Los Angeles have lot to offer, they have wide variety, places like Gaam to places like Star Night. Star Night is more class compared to Gaam and what standout from this place is Outdoor seating and great food.
The outdoor seating is vert pleasant on a nice day, they have very good heater lamps which made it cozier. Location is very convenient and right in the center of the K-Town. Also we ordered Kimchi Rice, , pork belly with kimchi, deep fried pork in sweet and sour sauce, spicy wings, asado, kimchi pasta and veggie options.
Drinks, we had hey have soju, sake, korean traditional wine, wine, bottled beer, and draft beer. Even their cocktails were decent.

Parking: Valet parking : $3
Free parking available around<//text>

< Text>
Although this says I've not been there for 7 months, I visit tobacco road frequently.
Product is excellent and well-cared-for.

The shop has a very welcoming feel to it and I think the shining star of the shop has to be the owner who is known as"Z".

He cares about his store, cares about his customers and he himself is a blast, just a really fun guy. Every single time I come in there, he puts a really big smile on my face and I always laugh out loud, sometimes at my own expense!

There are many shops in the Sacramento area that you can visit, this place has that extra something that I think you will love as I do.
They carry cigar products and also pipes and pipe tobacco. All of it is very good quality.  No cheap quality stuff in this store.

P.S. They are open for business now and if I were you, if you need any of these things, I would go visit. I highly recommend this business.</Text>

< text>
Very good selection of cigars in the spacious walk-in humidor.  They also have a selection of infused cigars if you are into that sort of thing.  Plenty of accessories to choose from, such as cutters, lighters, humidors.  Very good selection of pipes and pipe tobaccos.  The smoking lounge has about a dozen comfortable leather chairs and a sofa that you can sink into while you puff on your stogie as well as some bar stool type chairs.  They also have a tv mounted on the wall with dvd player for your viewing pleasure.  The guys who work there are friendly and knowledgable and are eager to help you pick out a cigar.</text>

< Review>
Very old hotel, no coffee in the room and no breakfast. The electric outlets did not work, paint was peeling from the walls leaving large bare spots. The water temperature in the bathroom was hot, hotter and hottest. The air conditioner was anemic. < Text>
I don't usually write reviews because it does take a lot of time and effort and I have kids... but my experience was so great I felt that it was my duty to let other parents know.

I took my 3 year old son to Ardary Family Dentistry for a second opinion. As soon as we walked in the dentist was ready to take him. I was able to sit with my son during the xrays and exam. They had him talking up a storm (very friendly dental assistants). There was a TV in the ceiling, which he thought was very cool and they gave him neat glasses and headphones. At one point my kid even grabbed the dentists mirror and he just laughed and said "hey that's mine".

He ended up needing three fillings (which was no where near the extensive work that the other dentist recommended) and I was so scared for him but my son had so much fun during the actual procedure I couldn't believe it. He has ZERO IDEA that he even got a shot to numb him and the entire process took no longer than 40 minutes! I couldn't believe it.

Going to the dentist can be very scary for a child especially if they need work done. I was so worried that he would be traumatized and I would have a hard time taking him back in the future..but he asked me to go back the next day?! He hit it off really well with the doc apparently. It is very comforting to know that there are still honest people out there that don‚Äôt ‚Äúoversell‚Äù What needs to be done (especially on children).< /Text>

< review>
Edit 2

I moved out of the Stanton location 2 months now and don't miss it one bit. My experience with Extra Space is the corporate office is very professional and polite but on site staff treat their customers bad. But it's the nature of the buisness. Corporate does alot in sales and treat people respectfully because of that side of a buisness as the location knows that they have to deal with a subset of people that may be in a tight spot. There are only a few reasons to have a storage, need the extra space, process of moving or down on you luck. But that is not a reason to look down on people in fact working at McDonald's takes skills and a storage employee is just under a janitor. But these guys lie to people they don't like like their unpublished undocumented rules they make if they don't like you. The other thing with Extra Space is they do not have a chain of command their district manager is the last say. Do yourself a favor and use a better storage company. One that gives you your lease, one that posts the rules, one that doesn't ask you for a review before you use their service. I used Stanton storage up the road for 8 years and that was from 2001 to 2009. Never did I have a problem. Never told one hour to do things once contact is signed none of Extra storage bs. No hidden rules and my rent only was raised twice during that time no one herrassed me and the people on the property never said anything negative. If you want to chance Extra Space especially the Stanton location do one thing ask people you see who currently rent what they ü§î because those months I rented there maybe 2 people had something positive to say out of maybe 20. Also this location is strange they know everything you do on property but they have lots of break in of the units but they know nothing. My guess is you work a dumb job yourvthe inside person that's my opinion.

Great price, fast and easy great service, this is an edit after 45 days of renting at this location he guy who rented me my unit I think is the manager he is a real good guy but but also doesn't listen ( I always hated a business that strong hands you to do a review before the service) I am disabled and have a service dog and was herrassed by the staff because of my dog for first 2 weeks and the are very unaware of the federal laws pertaining to service dogs. But after I finally had it with the constant herrassment of 1 staff member that is mentioned in reviews I then was harrassed on anything and everything. I was looked out from gate access before 30 days and now my unit is locked and restricted access.
